  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_153f3e69-ea8d-4ccf-bfb3-13f831d30c20'
      });

  <span id="freeText14884054914020357947" style="display:none"><b>This seductive paranormal series continues with a brutal Highland werewolf and an exquisite young witch, adversaries with a blood vendetta between them.</b><br /><br /><b>Her breathless kiss haunts him...</b><br /><br />Bowen MacRieve of the Lykae clan was nearly destroyed when he lost the one woman meant for him. The ruthless warrior grew even colder, never taking another to his bed—until a smoldering encounter with his enemy, Mariketa the Awaited, reawakens his darkest desires. When sinister forces unite against her, the Highlander finds himself using all his strength and skill to keep her alive.<br /><br /><b>His slow, hot touch is irresistible...</b><br /><br />Temporarily stripped of her powers, Mari is forced to take refuge with her sworn adversary. It's rumored that no one can tempt Bowen's hardened heart, but soon passion burns between them. Though a future together is impossible, she fears he has no intention of letting her go.<br /><br /><b>No deed is too wicked for her seduction...</b><br /><br />If they defeat the evil that surrounds them, can Mari deny Bowen when he demands her body and soul—or will she risk everything for her fierce protector?</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1588717167" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1588717167?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio 9781442354289" href="/book/show/13546129-wicked-deeds-on-a-winter-s-night">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of paranormal romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dangerous-hero-themed-books-read">dangerous-hero-themed-books-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1588717167" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9457867163308995714">I am totally addicted to this series! Each book only serves to suck me into this story further. Who knew that crossing supernatural beings would be so hot!<br/><br/>This fourth book in the 'Immortals After Dark' series, tells the story of Bowen and Mari, a werewolf and a powerful witch. From the start, their relationship is contentious. Bowen's family has a long and bitter rivalry with witches.<br/><br/>When Bowen begins to feel an attraction toward Mari, he assumes that she has cast a spell on him. After all, he's</span>
  <span id="freeText9457867163308995714" style="display:none">I am totally addicted to this series! Each book only serves to suck me into this story further. Who knew that crossing supernatural beings would be so hot!<br /><br />This fourth book in the 'Immortals After Dark' series, tells the story of Bowen and Mari, a werewolf and a powerful witch. From the start, their relationship is contentious. Bowen's family has a long and bitter rivalry with witches.<br /><br />When Bowen begins to feel an attraction toward Mari, he assumes that she has cast a spell on him. After all, he's spent years suffering after the loss of his "mate" following a tragic accident. Never in all those years had he felt an attraction to another, so he knows that the witch must be up to something.<br /><br />Believed to be the most powerful witch in her coven, Mari is just beginning to harness her power. She's led a sheltered life and has been abandoned by everyone she ever loved. She can't deny her attraction to the sexy werewolf, but she refuses to be second-best again. <br /><br />Eventually, Bowen cannot fight his attraction any longer. He has to choose between the love that was, and the love that could be. Once he sets out to win Mari over, he's got his work cut out for him. He'll have to work doubly hard to undo the damage he's already done.<br /><br />Just when things start to work out for these two, everything gets turned upside down. There were some pretty big twists that I didn't see coming. In my opinion, this book contains the most surprising plot twists in the series, so far.<br /><br />Overall, I enjoyed every minute of this story. It was fun and sexy, with a great storyline. More and more, I'm beginning to draw connections between all of the characters from the different books. <br /><br />I listened to the Audible version and the narration was great. Bowen's Scottish accent was sexy as hell! I highly recommend the audiobook. I'll be starting the next one immediately.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9457867163308995714" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_300376314" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/300376314" />
    <a title="Exina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5309539-exina"><img alt="Exina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580809437p2/5309539.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/300376314?book_show_action=true">Mar 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Exina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Exina" href="/user/show/5309539-exina">Exina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=can-be-read-as-a-stand-alone">can-be-read-as-a-stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=fae-fairies">fae-fairies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=heroes-i-want-for-myself">heroes-i-want-for-myself</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=laugh-out-loud-funny">laugh-out-loud-funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=sirens">sirens</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=likeable-heroine">likeable-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=guatemala">guatemala</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer300376314" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16827486687203355569"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I still don’t see why we couldn’t sleep in that cave,” Mari said as MacRieve led her out into the night.<br/>“Because my cave’s better than their cave.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>I’ve read the first 8 installments of the <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series, and so far Bowen and Mariketa’s book is my favorite.<br/><br/><i>Wicked Deeds on a Winter’s Night</i> overlaps the final events of the Talisman’s Hie, from Bowen and Mariketa’s perspective. Bowen traps Mariketa and other immortals in a tomb in the jungle of Guatemala, but Mariketa mana</span>
  <span id="freeText16827486687203355569" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I still don’t see why we couldn’t sleep in that cave,” Mari said as MacRieve led her out into the night.<br>“Because my cave’s better than their cave.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>I’ve read the first 8 installments of the <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series, and so far Bowen and Mariketa’s book is my favorite.<br><br><i>Wicked Deeds on a Winter’s Night</i> overlaps the final events of the Talisman’s Hie, from Bowen and Mariketa’s perspective. Bowen traps Mariketa and other immortals in a tomb in the jungle of Guatemala, but Mariketa manages to cast a spell on him before he leaves her there.<br><br>As you know from <i>No Rest for the Wicked</i>, Bowen <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[loses the Hie <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. As his injuries are not healing because of Mariketa’s spell, and the House of Witches threatens the whole Lore with a war because of the missing Mariketa, Bowen soon is on his way back to the jungle to free her.<br><br>It is a very exciting part of the series. The world of the Lore is revealed in more details: its inhabitants, rules, myths, and relations. The story represents deep emotions, hard choices, incredible twists, destiny, prophecy, magic, passion, adorable characters, and sparkling dialogues.<br><br>I loved Bowen and Mariketa’s (not only) verbal archness with each other. Mariketa is fated to Bowen, and he is also unique for her, because he fulfills the prophecy given to Mariketa. He is a catalyst for her magic, and able to control her power and protect Mariketa, even from herself.<br><br>The ending is completely astonishing. I was so engaged in the action of the story, as Bowen and Mariketa continually fight with each other, save each other, and fight for each other, that I simply didn’t see what was coming, and I was just shocked by the limitless cruelty and evil of the antagonist.<br><br>I'm totally in love with Bowen, the "shameless, tricksy wolf". He is vehement, ferocious, sometimes surly, but passionate and very gentle. He suffers from his guilt and pain because of the death of his mate, Mariah; struggles with his several centuries-old prejudices toward witches, and his doubt whether he is given another mate.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469653723i/19841368._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <i>He was so… wolfy. So teasing. And Mari realized this was kind of fun. She half-expected him to play-trip her and start nipping at her ears. And she suspected she’d love it.</i>
</blockquote><br>Mariketa, "the wee, bloody witch" is an amazing character. She is a brave, sensual, devious, and a very young woman with infinite but volatile power and strong principles. I admire her bravery, and forgiving attitude. She is also extremely powerful: she is s supposed to have powers from all fives castes of witches – the powers of a warrior, conjurer, seeress, enchantress, and healer.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469653723i/19841367.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The secondary characters are hilarious, especially Rydstrom, Nïx, and Carrow.<br><blockquote>
  <i>"How in the hell could you have gotten here so quickly?"<br>"Missed you, witch. Ran headlong. Now hang up the bloody phone."<br>"Oh, great Hekate, is that his voice?" Carrow cried. "I just had an orgasm!"</i>
</blockquote> <br>And the ending is so sweet...<br><blockquote>
  <i>"So that’s how we’re tae play this, wife?” Bowen said, when her snowball beaned him squarely in the face. He shook the snow from him in that wolfy way she loved. “You challenge a master at your own peril and have been duly warned.”<br>She wiggled her gloved fingers at him. “Bring it on, Father Time.”<br>But her eyes widened as he began piling up the biggest snowball she’d ever seen. She took off, darting back toward the lodge.<br>Playing in the snow—what an incredible way to end an already wonderful day. </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1565887648i/27998745.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://exinasreadings.tumblr.com/tagged/Wicked-Deeds-on-a-Winter%E2%80%99s-Night" rel="nofollow noopener">My favorite quotes.</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16827486687203355569" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25550790-wicked-deeds-on-a-winter-s-night">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer927905105" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17991504229190378307"><b>
  <blockquote>“Darwin says people like you need to die.” </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1482763942i/21546960._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Despite the fact that the whole story of Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night isn't my cuppa after all, I still loved every character Kresley Cole put into this book. Bowen was such a jerk for me when I first met him, he treats Mariketa so bad I wanted to kick his ass then. Mari, on the other hand, is genorous, lovely and tender. She is that type of heroine who is always hurt by a coldhearted hero. I pitied her so damn much and don't understand why I ga</span>
  <span id="freeText17991504229190378307" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“Darwin says people like you need to die.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1482763942i/21546960._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Despite the fact that the whole story of Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night isn't my cuppa after all, I still loved every character Kresley Cole put into this book. Bowen was such a jerk for me when I first met him, he treats Mariketa so bad I wanted to kick his ass then. Mari, on the other hand, is genorous, lovely and tender. She is that type of heroine who is always hurt by a coldhearted hero. I pitied her so damn much and don't understand why I gave this book five stars even though it's not my taste.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Damn it, MacRieve, if you keep calling me kitten, then I'm going to start calling you something equivalent, like hound dog - and then we'll both be losers.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482763942ra/21546961.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maybe it's because of the dynamic between the main characters that beat me up, or the sex scenes being so damn hot I fanned my face all the time while I was reading. Anyway, the second half of Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night was unexpectedly awesome after the crap of you-are-not-my-mate-but-I-still-want-you plot in the beginning almost bumped me off. The book finally redeemed itself with the conclusion so well I had to give it five stars.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Bashful? She and her friends made Girls Gone Wild look like a quilting circle.”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br>Oh ! Have I already told you that I loved Bowen for some parts of him ? He's flat out hot. SO DAMN HOT that I didn't care about his jerky and silly characteristic at all. It's just that. I'm so biased when it comes to Kresley Cole's books.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1482763942ra/21546962.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/882ndJ">https://goo.gl/882ndJ</a></span>

<div id="review_2008871020" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2008871020" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2008871020?book_show_action=true">May 24, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=witches-wizards">witches-wizards</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=valkyrie">valkyrie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=wolves-lycans">wolves-lycans</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2008871020" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16463520379084111056"><b>Bowen MacRieve, Lykae & Mariketa the Awaited, Witch</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“You could almost make me forget what I really want.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>1200 years old Lykae Bowen has known exactly what he wants for a few centuries now.<br/>And this is definitely <u>NOT</u> the 23 years old <u>distracting, distrusting and destructing witch</u> Mariketa.<br/><br/>His only goal is getting back to winter of 1827 and save his mate who run away from him during a full moon night when she saw his monster and she was killed by an accident. <br/>His <u>beautiful, fragile, perfect, fae</u></span>
  <span id="freeText16463520379084111056" style="display:none"><b>Bowen MacRieve, Lykae &amp; Mariketa the Awaited, Witch</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“You could almost make me forget what I really want.”</i>
</b><br /><br />1200 years old Lykae Bowen has known exactly what he wants for a few centuries now.<br />And this is definitely <u>NOT</u> the 23 years old <u>distracting, distrusting and destructing witch</u> Mariketa.<br /><br />His only goal is getting back to winter of 1827 and save his mate who run away from him during a full moon night when she saw his monster and she was killed by an accident. <br />His <u>beautiful, fragile, perfect, fae princess</u> Mariah.<br /><br />Lonely desperate Bowen has spent the last centuries in misery and sorrow, without a purpose in his life until he discovered the Hie competition -where the majority of the Lore factions are represented. The ultimate prize is the key to go back in time and he has to have it. Moreover Nyx has predicted that this competition is the key in order to get his mate.<br /><br />Mariketa –although she is still young and still not an immortal- wants to have the key as well, mainly to prove a point. There is no way this REALLY OLD, wolf-like, scary Scotish is going to stop her. No matter how much attracted she is to him. Anyway, he mourns for his lost mate. And there is no way Mariketa will be a second choice for anyone ever again! Plus the fact that she hates him since Bowen locked her up with a few immortals and many incubus demons in a dark cave without food and water for weeks.<br /><br />This is a story of <br />-<b>deception</b> where even the strongest wolf could be played by a cunning witch<br />-<b>lost love</b> that can make the strongest wolf weak when it is a fake, but it can also make the strongest wolf even stronger when it is the real thing<br />-<b>finding yourself and your purpose in life</b> even if it means that you have to destroy someone much stronger than you and that you may destroy yourself at the process and you will never be yourself again.<br />- <b>the fact that a Lykae/wolf is truly an animal</b> and sometimes this fact can be really handy.<br /><br />This is surely my favourite book so far in the series. It can be read in so many different levels.<br />It is passionate (hooray!!! for the wolves), funny, packed with adventure but equally packed with devastating drama and painful truth. <br /><b>It is a good thing that true love always wins!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16463520379084111056" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16191196904096752684">What can I say that hasn't been said? Loved it, almost as much as the previous book, "No Rest for the Wicked". If you enjoy sexual tension and sexual bantering in your books, this read will not disappoint! And when the H/H FINALLY get down to it--yowza!<br/><br/>Loved the hero, Bowen, although at first it was hard to read the Scottish accent, but I endured, and then the accent became downright sexy! And so far Mari is my favorite heroine of the IAD series. She was funny, brave, and good at putting the oft</span>
  <span id="freeText16191196904096752684" style="display:none">What can I say that hasn't been said? Loved it, almost as much as the previous book, "No Rest for the Wicked". If you enjoy sexual tension and sexual bantering in your books, this read will not disappoint! And when the H/H FINALLY get down to it--yowza!<br /><br />Loved the hero, Bowen, although at first it was hard to read the Scottish accent, but I endured, and then the accent became downright sexy! And so far Mari is my favorite heroine of the IAD series. She was funny, brave, and good at putting the often arrogant and cock-sure Bowen in his place! Fabulous ending, too. Made me reach for the next one in the series, and started reading it immediately!</span>

<div id="review_945172183" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945172183" />
    <a title="Sammy Loves Books" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14227114-sammy-loves-books"><img alt="Sammy Loves Books" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534119573p2/14227114.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/945172183?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sammy Loves Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sammy Loves Books" href="/user/show/14227114-sammy-loves-books">Sammy Loves Books</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal Romance Fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=library-book">library-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=bad-ass-heroine">bad-ass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=he-owns-my-heart">he-owns-my-heart</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=do-me-baby">do-me-baby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=lendable">lendable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=werewolves-rule">werewolves-rule</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer945172183" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11633955902735166730"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401972673i/9876088.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='bespelled wolf' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>"For one hundred and eighty years I've no' touched another" …"Have never even given a woman a second look. And it was <i>easy</i> to do so. But now I canna seem to keep my hands off a slip of a <i>witch</i>", he rasped at her ear. "A witch who has me feeling like I'll die if I doona find out what it'd be like to kiss her."…<i>"O' course it's a goddamned spell."</i>
</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><br/><b>Bowen MacRieve</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402538765i/9951758._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='560' alt='bowen' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Bowen is a werewolf that lost his mate one hundred and eighty years ago as she was fleeing him. He blames himself for her death and has</span>
  <span id="freeText11633955902735166730" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401972673i/9876088.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="bespelled wolf" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>"For one hundred and eighty years I've no' touched another" …"Have never even given a woman a second look. And it was <i>easy</i> to do so. But now I canna seem to keep my hands off a slip of a <i>witch</i>", he rasped at her ear. "A witch who has me feeling like I'll die if I doona find out what it'd be like to kiss her."…<i>"O' course it's a goddamned spell."</i>
</blockquote>
</b><br><br><br><b>Bowen MacRieve</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402538765i/9951758._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="560" alt="bowen" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Bowen is a werewolf that lost his mate one hundred and eighty years ago as she was fleeing him. He blames himself for her death and has lost all desire to live. He's lost weight and drinks too much alcohol. Bowen has not touched nor had desire for another, until meeting Mariketa.<br><br><br><b>Mariketa the Awaited</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402614419i/9960815.jpg" width="400" height="225" alt="cloke" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mariketa is a young witch, only twenty-three years old. She hasn't grown into her immortality yet but she has just entered The Talisman's Hie. It's a treacherous scavenger hunt amongst immortals and she wants to represent her coven well. But there is a prophecy that Mari's mate will take her away from her coven and keep her locked away. So she hides herself under a hooded cloak and changes her appearance with a glamour spell. <br><br><br>Yeah, that cloak is a total buzz kill. No one buys her drinks at karaoke night and it's hard to meet men when no one can check you out. Men are so visual. But Bowen can't seem to keep his eyes off her, even under that cloak. And the feeling is mutual. He's a hottie of a werewolf that has been mourning his mate. But he is fine as hell with his dark hair and amber eye and his Scottish accent is delicious. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402701424i/9974751.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="Mari" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Bowen has entered the competition in hopes of winning a key that will allow him to go back in time and save his mate. But when Mariketa and Bowen end up trapped in a cave and her cloak is removed, Bowen is unable to resist her any longer.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>She suddenly knew two things: He was about to kiss her so fiercely she would never be the same again.<br>And he would hate himself for it afterward and despise her forever.</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384707737ra/6936522.gif" width="400" height="196" alt="passion kiss" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>These two have a passion that they can not deny. Bowen is feeling guilty for desiring Mari, but he suspects that she has be-spelled him. Mariketa is young, but she is also very powerful. Did she unknowingly place a lust spell on Bowen? Or is there something more sinister going on?<br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402025004ra/9884169.gif" width="400" height="152" alt="kissing" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>This book was fast paced, full of action, explosions, and a very lusty werewolf. I am enjoying this series tremendously but I hope the next books have more external conflict between the main couple and less internal conflict. The first four books have plotted enemies to fall in love with mortal enemies. <br><br>It was fun for a few books but I am getting tired of it. We've had a vampire hating valkyrie fall in love with a vampire, a vampire hating werewolf fall in love with a vampire, and a witch hating werewolf fall in love with a witch. Enough already!! <br><br>Thank goodness the next book is about a Vampire and a Ghost. They are not mortal enemies. Should be fun!!!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> </blockquote>
</b><br><br><br><b>My Immortals After Dark Reviews:<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945149690" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945169131" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/949584205" rel="nofollow noopener">No Rest for the Wicked</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945172183" rel="nofollow noopener">Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945172557" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Needs at Night's Edge</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945172787" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dark Desires After Dusk</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/994211489" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of a Demon King</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945174408" rel="nofollow noopener">Untouchable</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945178167" rel="nofollow noopener">Pleasure of a Dark Prince</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945180198" rel="nofollow noopener">Demon from the Dark</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945180215" rel="nofollow noopener">Dreams of a Dark Warrior</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1289048120" rel="nofollow noopener">Lothaire</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1400296552" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Skye</a></b></span>

<div id="review_318404225" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/318404225" />
    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/318404225?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6563748-wicked-deeds-on-a-winter-s-night">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Kristen by: </span>
      Karla
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=lots-of-bickering">lots-of-bickering</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=humorous">humorous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=great-ending">great-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-characters">fabulous-characters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer318404225" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10888803616854976623"><b>4 to 4 1/2 stars</b><br/><br/>I thoroughly enjoyed reading <i>Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night</i>, the fourth book in the Immortals After Dark series. I was not as enamored with this story as I was with the third book, but I had fun reading it just the same. <br/><br/>The hero, Bowen, is one of the most tortured heroes I've read, yet he is genuine, likable and charming in a brusque way. His protective, consuming, and voracious nature toward his mate Mariketa, the heroine, was awe-inspiring and endearing. I truly adore Bowen'</span>
  <span id="freeText10888803616854976623" style="display:none"><b>4 to 4 1/2 stars</b><br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed reading <i>Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night</i>, the fourth book in the Immortals After Dark series. I was not as enamored with this story as I was with the third book, but I had fun reading it just the same. <br /><br />The hero, Bowen, is one of the most tortured heroes I've read, yet he is genuine, likable and charming in a brusque way. His protective, consuming, and voracious nature toward his mate Mariketa, the heroine, was awe-inspiring and endearing. I truly adore Bowen's character. <br /><br />The heroine, Mariketa (Mari), is a fantastic and fun character. I loved her spunk and determination but also her vulnerability and insecurity. She is my favorite heroine in the series thus far. I loved her. <br /><br />The plot twist at the end of this book took me by utter surprise. I honestly did not see the turn of events coming. <i>How awesome is that?!</i> I love when an author has the ability to surprise me. <br /><br />My only complaint about this book–and the series–and reason for the slight drop in rating is the annoying relationship pattern I've noticed in the books I've read thus far. In each book the hero and heroine continually banter with each other, which is fun and would be fine, if they–but mostly the heroine–didn't also continue to fight their attraction and inevitable relationship until the last few chapters of book. Since it's obvious Ms. Cole is a gifted and creative writer I can only hope she rectifies this relationship pattern in future books. <br /><br />Other than that, I can't seem get enough of this fantastic series, full of colorful, unique, fascinating, and compelling characters. One things for sure, Kristley Cole has created one captivating and exciting mythical world.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10888803616854976623" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<div id="review_2134438213" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2134438213" />
    <a title="Kaila" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35924884-kaila"><img alt="Kaila" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1533304308p2/35924884.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2134438213?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kaila" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kaila" href="/user/show/35924884-kaila">Kaila</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=hate-to-love">hate-to-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=2017">2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=angels-and-demons">angels-and-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=swoon-worthy-love-interest">swoon-worthy-love-interest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=vampires-and-shapeshifters">vampires-and-shapeshifters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2134438213" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11864027601784332792"><b>3.5/5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>“You could almost make me forget what I really want.” </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Yay!! My first ever <i>Kresley Cole</i> book...and it was <b>FANTASTIC!</b> This was a completely addicting book that I flew through.<b> I just couldn't get enough!</b> I admit, I probably should have started at book one so I knew the gist of all the worldbuilding and different creatures; but I still understood the book relatively well. Bowen and Mari's relationship was a rollercoaster of angst, misunderstandings and some serious sexual tension...b</span>
  <span id="freeText11864027601784332792" style="display:none"><b>3.5/5 stars</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>“You could almost make me forget what I really want.” </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Yay!! My first ever <i>Kresley Cole</i> book...and it was <b>FANTASTIC!</b> This was a completely addicting book that I flew through.<b> I just couldn't get enough!</b> I admit, I probably should have started at book one so I knew the gist of all the worldbuilding and different creatures; but I still understood the book relatively well. Bowen and Mari's relationship was a rollercoaster of angst, misunderstandings and some serious sexual tension...but <b>I loved it</b>. Apart they were great characters but together, they were near perfect. Now that I've gotten a taste for this series I know that I'm not going to be able to hold myself back!<br /><br />Mariketa and Bowen are both competing a magical competition, with the prize being the ability to go back in time twice. Mari is a young witch who has been prophesied to have great powers, only she's not quite there yet. She is competing for her Coven, and with the hope of unlocking some of this power that supposedly awaits her. Bowen is competing for a very different reason. He must go back in time to save his mate, the very one that he killed thousands of years before. In this magical and fantastical world, mates are bound so tightly that it is almost impossible to live once a mate dies. This is why Bowen wants to find a way to bring his mate back, in order to stop this agony that is eating him alive. The only problem is, he is feeling attracted to the young witch, even if he believes himself to be faithful to his dead mate.<br /><br />After an accident during the competition, Mari finds herself with Bowen, the very man that could have caused her death. Now, she must rely on him to help them get back to safety. This is especially hard when Bowen is persistent in treating Mari like his mate, which was his only explanation for the powerful attraction he felt for her. But Mari doesn't want to be used in that way, so she tries to stifle her feelings for Bowen, unless he decides that she is really his mate. However, romance is not the only thing on the table in her life, with a very powerful and evil force trying to destroy the coven and essentially her world. Mari must find a way to unlock her powers, but if she does this, will she still have time for Bowen; a Lykae who hates witches.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>“Damn it, MacRieve, if you keep calling me kitten, then I'm going to start calling you something equivalent, like hound dog - and then we'll both be losers.”</b>
</blockquote><br /><br />The romance in this book was <b>downright electrifying</b>. Despite a seriously rocky start and a very adversarial relationship, Bowen and Mira were undeniably attracted to each other. The sexual chemistry between this pair was<b> off-the-charts</b>, and was introduced in the first few chapters of the novel. I was <b>physically pained</b> just wanting these characters to get together already, but let me tell you, it was totally worth it when they did. The characters were totally different, but somehow together they were just perfect. Not only was it a very hot and sexy relationship, but they also had many sweet moments. This greatly contrasted the asshole-ish actions that Bowen showed towards Mari in the beginning, which I didn't exactly appreciate. Nonetheless, by the end of the book, I was fully invested in their romance which was both <b>greatly emotional and very sexually driven.</b><br /><br />I admit, there was quite a large portion of the book where I was quite confused as to what was happening. I'm not sure whether this is because I jumped right into the series without reading previous books, or the world building didn't connect to me. I'd say that the whole competition at the start didn't resonate with me. Nonetheless, after this moment I seemed to connect more to the characters and so I was less focused on the direction of the plot. This book was so <b>character driven</b>, and I'd take a guess that the whole series is similar. The plot was interesting, don't get me wrong, but the relationships were what really kept me going. In saying this, towards the climax at the end, I was fully invested in the story and I was dying to know the outcome. This slow connection to the plot did prevent me from enjoying the story early on, but it didn't really ruin my reading experience altogether.<br /><br />I'm most excited about exploring this series further because there is such an <b>elaborate, fantastical world </b>that I'm just dying to get to know. There are so many different creatures with internal politics, wars, animosity and allies. I saw a little snippet of this in the book, guy I'm sure that it will only get more intense as the series continues. I think this is <b>the most detailed paranormal book that I have ever read, </b>and this is only the beginning.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>“What’s your favorite place to visit?” He absently answered, “Wherever you are.” <br />“Bowen, five things about you can’t all be about me.” <br />But you’re the only good thing that I’ve got.” </b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="11864027601784332792" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText15437563452491597271" style="display:none">I loved this book!! I fell in love with Bowe in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_" title="A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a> and since then I've wanted him to get his happy ending.     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1103481913" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1103481913" />
    <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads"><img alt="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396922701p2/4561998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1103481913?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads">Carmel (Rabid Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio 9781442354289" href="/book/show/13546129-wicked-deeds-on-a-winter-s-night">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Carmel (Rabid Reads) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/2806016-melanie">Melanie</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio-2014">audio-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio">audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103481913" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17578103835156591582"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2015/04/audiobook-review-wicked-deeds-on-a-winters-night-by-kresley-cole.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br/><br/>Until this installment I didn’t realize that many of the plots in this series run parallel to each other, so when I found myself back in the midst of the Hie I was ecstatic. It was interesting finding out what happened to Bowen after Sebastian trapped him, and learning more about the witch who cursed him. The two protagonists played a wonderfully devious game of cat and mouse throughout WICKED DEEDS ON A WINTER’S NIGHT which made their dialogue hysterically funny, and th</span>
  <span id="freeText17578103835156591582" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2015/04/audiobook-review-wicked-deeds-on-a-winters-night-by-kresley-cole.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br /><br />Until this installment I didn’t realize that many of the plots in this series run parallel to each other, so when I found myself back in the midst of the Hie I was ecstatic. It was interesting finding out what happened to Bowen after Sebastian trapped him, and learning more about the witch who cursed him. The two protagonists played a wonderfully devious game of cat and mouse throughout WICKED DEEDS ON A WINTER’S NIGHT which made their dialogue hysterically funny, and their lovemaking mercurial, especially when MacRieve accidentally screamed his ex’s name. I had a blast listening to this title; Kresley Cole &amp; Robert Petkoff are a powerhouse of audiobook wizardry!<br /><br />Thus far, we’ve become versed in the intricate Lore surrounding this author’s Valkyries, vampires, and werewolves, so you’d be right to infer that my expectations vis-à-vis her witches were through the roof. Mariketa’s also part fey which means that Cole had heaps of awesome new material to work with, and rest assured that none of it was wasted. I loved discovering the powers related to the five casts, exploring the specifics surrounding the Awaited’s prophecy, and the captromancer powers were just plain cool (and creepy!). Other than a bit of glamour, and a couple of secondary characters, the fey elements were negligible which I’m assuming was intentional, and will be explored in a future installment.<br /><br />I liked how dissimilar the two protagonists were; Mari is only twenty-two years old, hasn’t been frozen into her immortality yet, and is the embodiment of a modern young woman. In comparison, Bowen is ancient, has already found &amp; lost his mate, and is prejudiced towards witches. Also, their relationship really got off on the wrong foot what with Mariketa cursing the werewolf, and MacRieve entombing her with crazed incubi. Watching these two attempt to bridge the gap was an exercise in futility, but when they finally give in to their baser instincts their chemistry was as clear as day. The twist at the end was exquisite, and I adored how it all came together.<br /><br />With only three IMMORTALS AFTER DARK installments under my belt, and still ten left to go (plus novellas), I risk repeating myself with regards to Robert Petkoff’s narration; however for the time being I’ve no shortage of positive adjectives to use when it comes to his delivery of this series. His sinfully dreamy Scottish accent was back for a second lap, and in addition to it he unleashed Bowen’s beast with a guttural werewolf voice that succeeded in doing naughty things to my insides. I’m sure that Petkoff captured Mari’s character beautifully as well, but for some strange reason all I can remember is MacRieve. RAWR!<br /><br />WICKED DEEDS ON A WINTER’S NIGHT’s title is self-explanatory or in other words… hot, hot, HOT!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17578103835156591582" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

This, combined with the fact that everyone expects greatness from her but so far she has only displayed volatile and uncontrollable powers make her want to prove that she can do better. She worked to get what she wanted and she let no-one walk all over her.<br><br>Bowen and Mariketa together where a time bomb but they were also perfect for each other. The book is of the usual "Cole" pattern, which translates to "Mariketa is a witch, Bowen hates witches more than any other Lore species but he can't resist her".   <i>The witch seethed with power. Spells and magicks swirled about her.</i>

I find myself liking the witches more than the valykrie, so this focusing on them was better for me.<br /> <br /><b>

</b><br /> <br />Bowen and Mari had a sweet but challenging connection that made them fun to read but again, the whole Bowen being a werewolf and NEEDING to claim his mate made the boners and sex OTT. I know a lot like this but it's a bit out of my realm.<br /> <br /><b>
  <i>All at once Mari understood why people fought losing battles---because if you want something badly enough, you can't do anything else but fight for it.</i>
</b><br /> <br />My favorite part of the story and what gave it an extra half star was the author's subtle inclusion of the idea that "monsters" are feeling beings too. From the incubi paying Mari to end them to Bowen at full werewolf pausing a moment before breaking down the door. It brought depth and feeling to the characters and world where monsters is definitely a shades of grey word.<br /> <br />Does this series have plans to go on forever because with the insane amount of characters and story offshoots, it feels like it could go on forever. <br />I cheated and looked ahead through the series to make sure Rydstrom gets a story after being introduced to him here. He does, book #5, and I MUST have it!</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781849834148" href="/book/show/9779851-wicked-deeds-on-a-winter-s-night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=casters-or-witches">casters-or-witches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=shifters-or-weres">shifters-or-weres</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=highlanders">highlanders</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1420380347" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3322551384912272160">Sorry that I have to do this for 2 books in a row, but I couldn't even remotely find anything to get fetish happy about...again. I can promise though that I DO have a plan for book 5's cafe scene. I'm halfway through 5 and it's already ticking off some boxes. So we <i>will</i> be getting back to the cafe. Soon.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444922044i/16574279.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In the meantime, you can can get acquainted with the series in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/367393428' rel='nofollow noopener'>Episode 1</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/260575073' rel='nofollow noopener'>Episode 2</a><br/><br/>First, a disclaimer : I didn't DISLIKE <i>Wicked Deeds</i>. I'm already such a fan of this author's quirky world and</span>
  <span id="freeText3322551384912272160" style="display:none">Sorry that I have to do this for 2 books in a row, but I couldn't even remotely find anything to get fetish happy about...again. I can promise though that I DO have a plan for book 5's cafe scene. I'm halfway through 5 and it's already ticking off some boxes. So we <i>will</i> be getting back to the cafe. Soon.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444922044i/16574279.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the meantime, you can can get acquainted with the series in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/367393428" rel="nofollow noopener">Episode 1</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/260575073" rel="nofollow noopener">Episode 2</a><br><br>First, a disclaimer : I didn't DISLIKE <i>Wicked Deeds</i>. I'm already such a fan of this author's quirky world and characters. The book was entertaining as hell. The story pacing was excellent. <br><br>But I didn't like the couple much as a couple. Bowen got on my nerves. The age difference between he and Mariketa was painfully awkward to read. You would think that the difference between innocent Emma and experienced Lachlain in <i>A Hunger Like No Other</i> had to be more of an obstacle, but it never was for me. Emma's sheltering almost helped her fit better into an immortal world. On the flip side, there was something always unmatched between Bowen and Mari that never quite popped into alignment. Mariketa was youthful and modern. Bowen was just cranky and old. I mean, I get it - he WAS old. But I need an author to sell me on the idea of a centuries (or millenia) old being able to keep up with modern times. And if he CAN'T, then I need to see him matched with someone better suited for him. <br><br>The Mariketa/Mariah story was a weird pairing. The end twist was clever, but I wasn't sure if the author had planned it that way all along, or if that idea came to her later. Something about the entire setup didn't flow as smoothly as it could have. <br><br>The book definitely had me feeling a like/dislike contradiction. But even as I count <i>Wicked Deeds</i> as my least favorite of the series so far, I still liked it better than a lot of books I've read. So we're still on the positive train here. I'm truly enjoying the series and am already zipping through book 5 like a madwoman. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3322551384912272160" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15329466-iliada?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15329466-iliada?shelf=highlander">highlander</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15329466-iliada?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15329466-iliada?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15329466-iliada?shelf=shape-shifters">shape-shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15329466-iliada?shelf=witches-wizards">witches-wizards</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15329466-iliada?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1042334026" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15778385673393864775"><b>All the stars in the sky for this book</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413649049ra/11540398.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It's been a year since I read the first book in the series. I seriously don't know why I've waited so long. When I read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_' title='A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Hunger Like No Other</a>, one of the best paranormals I've ever read, I thought that it was the best this series had to offer. The third book wasn't that good so this only confirmed my belief. How could anyone surpass Lachlain? Well, Bowen was just as good!<br/><br/>Silly me! People had told me about the MacRieves in this series! Why do I never listen?</span>
  <span id="freeText15778385673393864775" style="display:none"><b>All the stars in the sky for this book</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413649049ra/11540398.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's been a year since I read the first book in the series. I seriously don't know why I've waited so long. When I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_" title="A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a>, one of the best paranormals I've ever read, I thought that it was the best this series had to offer. The third book wasn't that good so this only confirmed my belief. How could anyone surpass Lachlain? Well, Bowen was just as good!<br><br>Silly me! People had told me about the MacRieves in this series! Why do I never listen? I know people will think that I just loved this because the hero is a Highlander. It's true, I adore the Scots, but that's not it. I mean, yes, those Lykae are seriously hot.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426502850i/14023550._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the Scotish brogue? Wow, it's such a turn-on for me. And the things Bowen said to Mariketa? OMG, they will have you all hot and bothered. But this book was just so intense!!This is a typical IAD book, with the enemies-to-lovers theme. Bowen hates the witches, he mistrusts Mariketa, but he wants her at the same time. They fight, they bicker, they play dirty. Their relationship?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419121932ra/12992189.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I just adore Mariketa too! This girl is amazing! She's clever, she's funny, she's brave! She won't allow Bowen to push her around. That's my girl! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426502670i/14023543.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are many funny moments! I was listening to this from my phone while walking and I burst into laughter. I had to pretend I was talking on the phone with somebody or people would think I'm crazy! And I love how modern all the heroines are in this series. Even those who are thousand years old. <br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Mari began to suspect that this reflection was going to prove to be like that little computer paperclip assistant -- at first it helps, but after a while you just want the paperclip to die.” </blockquote>
</i><br><br>It's really funny. Oh and Nix!<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“She, too, is one of Regin’s friends. They’re poker buddies, sisters of the Wii, and Mari is a vaunted member of the karaoke contingent. Regin has long acted as the witches’ designated driver.” “BFF?” Lachlain asked, brows drawn. “Sisters of the what?” <br>Emma supplied, “Best friend forever and a video game.” <br>Lachlain muttered to Emma, “Your relatives are just no’ right.” </blockquote>
</i><br><br>One more reason I was reluctant to read this book was that I was somehow left with the impression that Bowen would be fixated on his first mate and stubbornly refuse to love the heroine until the end. Nope! He wanted Mariketa from the beginning and it didn't take him long to realise that she suited him better than his first mate.<br><br>This book was perfect and so sweet.<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“What’s your favorite place to visit?” He absently answered, “Wherever you are.” <br>“Bowen, five things about you can’t all be about me.” <br>But you’re the only good thing that I’ve got. </blockquote>
</i><br><br>I'm really sad to see it end. I don't expect that all the books in the series will be that good, it's not possible, but I'll not make the same mistake again. I'll keep reading and maybe I'll be lucky.<br><br><i>P.S.: The narrator of the audiobook is amazing! He does all the accents perfectly and the females sound natural too! I was drooling over Bowen and I really loved Rydstrom and Cade's accents as well.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="15778385673393864775" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_347829007" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/347829007" />
    <a title="D.G." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/210123-d-g"><img alt="D.G." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1330353755p2/210123.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/347829007?book_show_action=true">Jun 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="D.G." class="user" itemprop="url" name="D.G." href="/user/show/210123-d-g">D.G.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781501120633" href="/book/show/25110911-wicked-deeds-on-a-winter-s-night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=awesome-narration">awesome-narration</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer347829007" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8056298655002429206"><b>Re-read Nov 2020</b> <br/>The more I read this book, the more I realize how uneven the story was. Bowen made mistake after mistake and poor Mariketa just kept forgiving him and giving him chances! That said, I understand why she did it...I think I can forgive Bowen everything because of that accent. God almighty! But that accent is hot. *fans self*<br/><br/><b>Re-read: Jan 2017</b><br/>This is the third time I re-read this book and it amazes me how my perspective changes between reads. This time, I understand the author gave </span>
  <span id="freeText8056298655002429206" style="display:none"><b>Re-read Nov 2020</b> <br />The more I read this book, the more I realize how uneven the story was. Bowen made mistake after mistake and poor Mariketa just kept forgiving him and giving him chances! That said, I understand why she did it...I think I can forgive Bowen everything because of that accent. God almighty! But that accent is hot. *fans self*<br /><br /><b>Re-read: Jan 2017</b><br />This is the third time I re-read this book and it amazes me how my perspective changes between reads. This time, I understand the author gave him lots of opportunities for growth (which he definitely needed.) I mean, who the hell thinks about trying to impregnate a woman the first time he sleeps with her?<br /><br />Something else I noticed in this re-read was how Mariketa took charge of her destiny. She was the one calling the shots during the mating and she had the big badass fight with the villain. Bowen was almost like her sidekick!<br /><br /><b>Re-read on audio 10/29/14:</b> This time around, I found Bowen <i>really</i> annoying. It was all about him, him, him and what <i>he</i> wanted. I really don't know how Mariketa kept giving him chances. I felt like stabbing him in the balls several times. Anywho, enjoyed it nevertheless...Petkoff is just too good on audio!<br /><br /><b>First read on Jun 2012</b><br />**3 stars for the story plus 1 bonus star for narration**<br /><br />I rarely read series books back to back but I was so obsessed with the narration that I couldn't wait any longer. I'm really glad the rest of the audiobooks in the series haven't been produced yet because I would probably be tempted to listen them all!<br /><br />Anyways, this story is very similar to the previous ones: man chases woman because he thinks she's his mate while the woman doesn't want anything to do with the guy, blah, blah, blah. But unlike the other books, the hero thinks the heroine (a witch) has enchanted him because he had already had a mate (who died) and men of his kind only get to have one. Regardless, he figures he should follow along because it's like he's getting a second chance.<br /><br />Bowen is really conflicted about his feelings for Mariketa, feeling disloyal to Mariah, his dead mate. I really enjoyed this part of the plot and was pleasantly surprised at how that was ultimately resolved. I only wished the author would have taken this chance to build a book that was a bit different than the others with the heroine chasing the hero for once. She had material to create such a plot.<br /><br />But my reason to picking this book wasn't really the story but the narration. The voice for Bowen was scrumptious, specially when he was in a charming frame of mind. The first time I heard him, my feelings were very similar to Carrow's:<br /><br />"Oh great Hekate, is that his voice?" Carrow cried "I just had an orgasm."<br /><br />I'm still just 'meh' on the series but I'll definitely keep listening as long as Mr. Petkoff is the narrator.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8056298655002429206" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=2012">2012</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer178123514" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer328778034016121237"><b>Edit: ReRead time....</b>*sigh* kresley cole has turned me into a polyamorous person. I mean i fall in love with every hero, I adore every heroine. I can't get enough. I wish i could go back in time and read all her stuff over, like an immortals after dark virgin...but i cant. so i will have to be content with rereads. STILL AMAZING. loved this book, who doesn't love a brooding lykae ...yummmmmmm<br/><br/><b>Wicked Deeds ona Winter's Night: 5 star read! <i>enjoyment</i> :)</b><br/><br/><br/><br/>I should review this. However, I devoured this </span>
  <span id="freeText328778034016121237" style="display:none"><b>Edit: ReRead time....</b>*sigh* kresley cole has turned me into a polyamorous person. I mean i fall in love with every hero, I adore every heroine. I can't get enough. I wish i could go back in time and read all her stuff over, like an immortals after dark virgin...but i cant. so i will have to be content with rereads. STILL AMAZING. loved this book, who doesn't love a brooding lykae ...yummmmmmm<br /><br /><b>Wicked Deeds ona Winter's Night: 5 star read! <i>enjoyment</i> :)</b><br /><br /><br /><br />I should review this. However, I devoured this book and it is 4 AM. I don't trust my brain! So here is a short list to suffice until i can be somewhat coherent and intelligent <br /><br />1. There is something about lykae. I mean, vampires are sex and so are faerie highlanders....but Lykae. So primal. So tortured. They want to provide, protect, and love. They are that simple yet add a blissful complexity to their mate. Bowe did that for me. I'd take a Lykae over a a vamp any day.<br /><br />2. This was such a fast read. It took me about 3-4 Hours! woooow! <br /><br />3. I liked how simple it was. The IAD books are so freaking complicated now with the hot mess state of the lore and ascension hooplah. It's fun to go back and read the books when it was just sexual tension and lots o love! :)<br /><br />4. Honestly, idk how good this book is in terms of literary merit. I'm just realizing that the steam was a teensy bit low, and some other flaws. However, i enjoyed it soooo much. Its like watching a good 80s movie. MAYBE the wardrobe and acting is a little sub par, but don't you just love it. Isn't your day brightened and your smile wide and genuine? At the end of the day, I think that's what makes a book a <i>goodread</i>... its that after glow of happiness that one can only achieve from a bajillion well strung together words and ideas that make up ...books!<br /></span>
